### 1. 第一人称视角：杭州用餐恶作剧

**作者**: [Emily](https://x.com/IamEmily2050/status/2043601704734659070)  **日期**: 2026-04-13  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Seedance 2.0 设计的详细第一人称视角视频提示词，包含角色互动以及在杭州西湖边对食物做出滑稽反应的场景。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/31fce9be3c01e3a8c88022accaf3b100/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/31fce9be3c01e3a8c88022accaf3b100/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
realistic live-action, single continuous shot, full first-person POV, no cuts, no angle changes, no scene transitions, no montage, no flash cuts, no music, no subtitles. Only two characters: my unseen first-person POV and @ Image1 sitting across from me. Natural ambient sound only: light restaurant noise, tableware, distant water, faint voices, chewing, spitting, rinsing, my laughter.

Setting:
Outdoor dining table beside West Lake, Hangzhou, near the water, calm daylight or soft late afternoon light. Real smartphone-video realism, grounded textures, realistic food, realistic body and hand motion, accurate chopstick use, accurate mouth movement, accurate eye focus. The lake stays visible to one side of frame.

Character:
@ Image1 is the only visible person. She can switch seamlessly between slightly fierce-cute and soft adorable. Lip sync, voice, expressions, and body language stay fully synchronized. Emotional arc: cheerful and relaxed while eating, then shocked disgust, then angry embarrassment.

Table:
Exactly 7 dishes on the table. One dish is the West Lake vinegar fish shown in @ Image2. @ Image1 is happily eating rice and the other dishes, but not the fish at first. The table feels full but readable. The fish dish remains clearly visible before I offer it to her.

Camera:
Entire video is from my seated first-person view across the table. My hand and chopsticks may enter frame naturally. Slight handheld micro-shake from breathing and laughter only, never chaotic. No third-person shots, no reverse shots, no overhead shots, no cutaways. Continuous believable framing centered on @ Image1 with part of the lake visible.

Action:
@ Image1 sits opposite me, happily eating from her bowl, enjoying rice and other dishes except the West Lake vinegar fish. She looks bright, playful, relaxed, cute.

From first-person POV, I pick up one bite of the fish with chopsticks and slowly extend it toward her. She notices it immediately, trusts me, leans forward, opens her mouth happily, and makes a cute “aam” sound as she bites the fish. I gently pull the chopsticks and my hand back out of frame.

She chews happily for about one second, expecting it to taste good. Then the taste hits. Her expression changes instantly into exaggerated but believable disgust. Her face shifts into a comedic purple-disgust reaction while staying within realistic live-action style. She quickly turns toward the lake and spits it out with repeated “ptui, ptui, ptui” sounds. The motion is fast, fluid, and continuous from chewing to rejection.

The moment she starts spitting, I begin laughing in first-person POV and keep laughing through the whole reaction. My laughter sounds genuine, amused, and uncontrollable, coming from behind the camera. The camera shakes slightly from laughing.

After spitting, @ Image1 sticks out her tongue in disgust, immediately grabs the water on the table
````

Then the room flickers into a completely different reality. 13-Second One-Take Sequence 0–2s The living room suddenly transforms into a horror scene, walls decayed, dim red lighting, distant whispering. Presses pause. Steps through the frozen scene. 12–13s They sit back into their original couch position. The room snaps back to normal. On TV: “Continue Watching?” Soft Netflix red glow fades. A 19-year-old woman with micro braids dyed deep indigo, warm brown skin, wearing a shredded athletic wrap top and cargo trousers - hook: extreme snap zoom to her eyes, pupils dilate, she exhales smoke in cold air, then launches a dynamic surge directly into frame. Combat takes place in an abandoned symmetrical library - towering bookshelves as leading lines, books exploding outward with every forceful impact, paper filling the air as environmental debris. Her movement vocabulary: rhythmic loops of continuous forward momentum, never retreating, each strike building on the last with no recovery given. Vertical stakes: shelves begin falling like dominoes, the fighters ascending the collapsing structure. Unexpected ending: she wins the exchange, opponent is down - she looks around at the total destruction, reaches into the rubble, pulls out a specific undamaged book, tucks it under her arm, and walks out through a hole in the wall. ### 5. 种子 —— 时间与尺度的演变

**作者**: [Cyber AI Creator 🎨](https://x.com/noman23761/status/2043006682402558439)  **日期**: 2026-04-11  **语言**: en

````
THE SEED — Amazon Rainforest, One Tree, All Time One impossible continuous shot. Through matter. Through scale. Through time. No cuts. [0s–2s] The camera floats in the canopy of the Amazon rainforest. Dense, dripping, impossibly green. Toucans call. Monkeys move through branches. The camera drifts downward through layers of leaves — each layer a different shade of green, a different species, a different world. Light falls in shifting patterns. [2s–4s] The camera reaches the forest floor. Dark, humid, teeming. A seed sits in the black soil — a Brazil nut, mahogany-colored, the size of a fist. The camera pushes in. Closer. Closer. It passes into the soil. Darkness. Roots thread through the earth like veins. Underground, the unseen network. [4s–6s] The camera shrinks. It enters the seed itself. Inside, cellular structures — green, geometric, pulsing with water. The camera witnesses germination in time-lapse. A root breaks through the seed coat. A shoot pushes upward. Cells divide in radial symmetry. Life organizes itself. [6s–8s] The shoot breaks the surface. The camera rises with it. Time accelerates. The seedling becomes a sapling. Rain falls in fast-motion streaks. The sapling thickens — a year per second. Branches extend. The trunk widens. Bark forms, furrows, hardens. A decade of growth in two seconds. [8s–11s] The tree is adult now. Enormous. The camera pulls back as the trunk widens to 3 meters across. The canopy spreads. Animals arrive — a sloth climbs the trunk, orchids bloom on the branches, a jaguar sleeps in a crook of the roots. An entire ecosystem built around one organism. The camera rises with the tree as it reaches for the canopy. [11s–13s] The tree breaks through the canopy ceiling. Sunlight. The camera emerges from the green into open sky. For the first time, the scale of the forest is visible — an unbroken ocean of green stretching to every horizon. Rivers thread through it like silver veins. Clouds build. The tree is one cell in a body the size of a continent. [13s–15s] The camera keeps rising. The Amazon basin curves with the Earth. The planet's edge appears. Blue atmosphere against black space. The forest is a green lung on a blue world. One seed. One tree. One forest. One planet. The same thing at every scale. Cut to black. Impossible continuous shot: canopy → soil → inside seed → germination time-lapse → tree growth → canopy emergence → continental aerial → orbital perspective. Lighting transitions from dappled green forest to dark underground to cellular bioluminescence to
````

### 7. 悬崖城市极速飞车追逐动作场景

**作者**: [Zara](https://x.com/ZaraIrahh/status/2042813595726029184)  **日期**: 2026-04-11  **语言**: en

> 这是一个极其详尽、多段式的动作提示词，用于生成一场穿梭于悬崖城市、瀑布和古老洞穴的连续长镜头飞车追逐。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c98c9346733b21ecb443b70e6641134a/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c98c9346733b21ecb443b70e6641134a/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
Speeder chase across a cliff city (single continuous shot) From a monumental cliffside city carved into stone, the camera dives toward a tiny streak of light ripping along a narrow ledge-road. Lock-on: a speeder hugging the wall at insane speed. The camera slingshots ahead, whips back, then drops tight to the rear thrusters: heat haze, grit snapping off the ledge, warning lights flashing. A collapsing balcony rains debris; the rider snaps a last-inch swerve under a falling arch, then threads through hanging laundry lines and open windows in one fluid line. The camera darts through the same openings, staying glued to the motion. One final bend and sudden calm: the camera blasts outward into a reveal of the city opening onto a boundless waterfall-fed valley, mist turning into rainbow.The rainbow mist lingers for half a second — serenity — then a SHADOW slices across it. From above, two black pursuit speeders dive through the mist, engines screaming. The camera tilts up just as the lead speeder banks hard off the cliff edge, skimming inches above the waterfall’s roaring drop. Spray explodes across the lens but never cuts. The camera rolls with the rider as they plunge straight down the waterfall face — not falling, but riding the vertical air current. Thrusters flare blue-white, stabilizers flickering. Pursuit crafts follow, firing pulse shots that streak through the mist like comets. The rider kicks sideways into a cavern hidden behind the waterfall curtain. The camera punches through liquid light into darkness — bioluminescent moss ignites along the cave walls, revealing an ancient tunnel carved by forgotten hands. Water drips in slow motion as the speed never drops. The camera swings low beneath the speeder, hugging the water-slick stone. Sparks burst as the underside grazes rock. Ahead: a broken bridge spanning a massive underground chasm. No slowdown. The rider guns it. The camera races ahead, flips 180° mid-air as the speeder launches the gap. For a breathless second, only void below — a bottomless abyss glowing faintly with magma veins. Mid-jump, one pursuer clips the edge and spirals down, vanishing into the darkness. The second clears it. Landing hard, the rider blasts toward a vertical shaft of daylight spearing down from above. The tunnel narrows — ancient gears and colossal stone mechanisms begin turning, triggered by the intrusion. Rotating rings. Crushing slabs.
````

**Prompt:**
````
生成一个青衣女子 图片1 在山间快速御剑飞行的第一人称视角（pov视角）视频画面从始至终都是第一人称视角。真人电影写实风格。模拟镜头为人物的眼睛，超现实pov视角（不出现主体实体和面部，仅出现剑），模仿镜头人物眼睛往下看再往远处眺望的感觉。镜头有极度的摇晃感和快速飞行的感觉。画面一：镜头模仿人物往下看，看见人物的鞋子和衣裙。画面二：镜头模仿人物往前看前方，镜头的高度模拟人的眼睛视角（不出现脚，鞋子，衣裙等人物的部分）看向前方，御剑飞行的画面。整体营造一个十分震撼的仙侠氛围。全程画面流畅，一镜到底，仅生成环境的音效，不要配背景音乐。注意剑的大小跟周围环境的比例正常和谐，两旁的高山非常大，人物很渺小。仅参考图片元素和环境，不是首尾帧模式。剑全程保持长度不变。仅通过镜头上摇和下摇更换视野角度。镜头的位置必须保持不变，必须模仿人物的第一人称pov视角
````

### 11. 变色龙打喷嚏喜剧短片

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/a24cc027640e1f555051be518911ccd3/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/a24cc027640e1f555051be518911ccd3/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
FORMAT: 12s / 1 Continuous Dolly Shot / Vibrant 3D Animation / Extreme Squash and Stretch SUBJECTS: A tiny, bug-eyed chameleon. A fluffy, yellow, pollen-covered butterfly. 
ENVIRONMENT: A lush, highly detailed tropical jungle branch. Warm sunlight filtering through green leaves. MOOD: Escalating panic, silent comedy, cartoon physics.  
TIMELINE:  0:00–0:03: Close-up. The chameleon is perfectly green, camouflaged against a large leaf. A fluffy, yellow butterfly floats down and lands directly on the tip of the chameleon's nose.  

0:03–0:07: The chameleon's eyes cross to look at the butterfly. It inhales deeply, trying to hold back a massive sneeze. Panic sets in. The chameleon loses control of its camouflage—its skin rapidly changes colors from green to neon pink, then to black-and-white zebra stripes.  

0:07–0:10: The internal pressure builds. The chameleon's body inflates like a round rubber balloon, its cheeks puffing out massively. The butterfly stays perfectly still on its nose.  

0:10–0:12: The sneeze! A powerful, sudden burst of air. The force of the sneeze launches the completely round chameleon backward off the branch like a rocket, leaving the butterfly spinning in mid-air in a cloud of glowing yellow pollen.
````

### 12. 女性特工电影级战斗提示词

![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/4f75ea331091a4098532e49a7bc1500d/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
Character
A highly trained female operative in a sleek black tactical suit, calm, focused, controlled breathing, sharp eyes scanning constantly.
Dual pistols in hand, precise and efficient.

0-3s
Camera starts inside a luxury bank.
Slow push through a tense standoff—security guards aiming, civilians frozen.
She stands in the center, perfectly still.

3-5s
Without warning—everything explodes into motion.

Transition through glass reflections.

11-13s
Massive push forward into main hall.
Camera pulls wide—chaos everywhere.
She moves through it like it’s slowed down.

13-15s
Final moment.
She exits through shattered glass doors into daylight.
Doesn’t look back.
Behind her—delayed impacts, everything collapses.
Camera freezes on her walking away.

Continuous tracking shot, tight proximity + dynamic orbit + whip transitions masked by movement
````

**Prompt:**
````
Ultra-refined motion design sequence. Absolute black background.
Monochrome white visual language with subtle accents of negative space.
Single continuous shot — no cuts, no camera movement.
All transformation emerges from the center.
Self-illuminated geometry, razor-sharp edges, no noise, no gradients.
0–1s [GENESIS]
A thin vertical white beam fades into existence at center frame.
It hums subtly, then splits into two parallel lines — perfectly symmetrical — before snapping back into one.
1–2s [FRACTURE]
The line fractures into multiple short segments, evenly spaced.
Each segment drifts slightly apart horizontally, creating a rhythmic broken-line pattern.
2–4s [WAVEFIELD]
The segments begin oscillating vertically in a sine-wave motion.
The wave propagates outward from center, forming a smooth, synchronized waveform across the frame.
4–6s [RIBBON → TORUS]
The waveform thickens into a continuous flowing ribbon.
It twists in 3D space, curling inward and seamlessly connecting into a rotating torus (donut shape), perfectly centered.
6–8s [TORUS → DATA RINGS]
The torus splits into multiple concentric rotating rings.
Each ring carries small evenly spaced white nodes, like data points orbiting in precise synchronization.
8–10s [NETWORK]
Thin lines connect the orbiting nodes across rings, forming a dynamic geometric network.
Connections appear and disappear algorithmically, suggesting intelligence and computation.
10–11.5s [COMPRESSION]
The entire network contracts inward.
Lines retract, nodes accelerate toward center, forming a dense glowing cluster.
11.5–13s [ENERGY CORE]
The cluster stabilizes into a pulsating polyhedral core — a clean geometric solid made of interconnected edges.
It rotates subtly, emitting faint rhythmic pulses.
13–14s [DISASSEMBLY]
The core disintegrates into perfectly straight radial lines shooting outward briefly — then reversing direction, snapping back inward.
14–15s [IDENTITY REVEAL]
All lines converge into a single horizontal baseline.
From this line, minimal white typography rises upward — forming the brand logo in a clean sans-serif.
A soft, brief glow radiates from below, then fades to pure black.
Style: futuristic minimalism, Swiss design precision, computational elegance
Mood: intelligent, controlled, inevitable, high-end tech brand identity
````

### 23. 超动态热带度假视频

**作者**: [GENEL | AIを用いた動画制作](https://x.com/genel_ai/status/2041452421591834708)  **日期**: 2026-04-07  **语言**: ja

> 这是为 Seedance 2.0 设计的一套高度详细、多段式的日语提示词，旨在创作一段关于年轻日本女性热带度假的超动态一镜到底风格视频。提示词详细规定了场景构图、人物动作（奔跑、进入别墅、跳入大海）、运镜（超动态跟拍、无缝转场）、光影（清澈的热带日光）以及色彩基调（青色、绿松石色、钴蓝色）。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/7d027431da19679374438f970f98f01b/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/7d027431da19679374438f970f98f01b/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
【コア・コンセプト：Ultimate Tropical Escape】

1. シーン構成とアクション (Scene & Action)
冒頭:

視点は、茶髪の日本人の20歳のかわいい女性の背後を追う三人称視点のトラッキングショット。
彼女は南国風のへそ出しキャミソールと、タイトなジーンズのホットパンツを合わせた洗練されたリゾートスタイルを着用し、ピンクのリモワ風アルミキャリーバッグを軽快に引いている。少し焼けた肌。
場所は、エメラルドグリーンの海の上に浮かぶ木製の桟橋（ウッドデッキ）。
彼女は期待を抑えきれないように、最初からかなり勢いよく前のめりに走り出す。
歩幅は大きく、足運びは非常に軽快で、キャリーバッグの車輪もスピードに合わせて小気味よく滑る。
髪とトップスの裾が風を受けてなびき、到着を待ちきれない高揚感が全身から伝わる。

中盤（ルームツアー）:

彼女がモダンな水上ヴィラの木製の扉を開けると、そこには広大なオーシャンビューが広がる。
カメラは彼女の動きに同期し、リビング、円形の通路、そしてバスルームへと途切れず高速で流れるように移動する。
彼女は室内に入ってからもスピードをほとんど落とさず、弾むような足取りで駆け抜ける。
まるで目的地へ一直線に吸い込まれていくような、期待感に満ちた動き。
部屋の途中で、彼女は走る勢いのままキャリーバッグのハンドルから自然にサッと手を離し、バッグは慣性で壁際へ滑るように流れ、静かに止まる。彼女は一切ためらわず、そのままさらに加速してテラスへ向かう。

クライマックス:

彼女はヴィラのテラスから外へ飛び出し、そのままほとんど減速せずに階段を駆け下り、迷うことなくターコイズブルーの海へとダイブする。
この時、彼女はすでに手ぶらで、両手を自由に広げながらジャンプする。
助走の勢いがそのまま空中へ抜けるような、大胆で伸びのあるジャンプ。
空中で手足を大きく広げ、水しぶき（スプラッシュ）が美しく舞い上がる瞬間を捉える。

2. 視覚的・技術的ディテール (Visual & Technical Details)
カメラワーク:
Hyper-dynamic follow shot: 被写体との距離を一定に保ちながら、ジンバルを使用したような揺れの少ない、しかし圧倒的なスピード感のあるトラッキング。
One-cut style: まるでワンカットで撮影されたかのようなシームレスなトランジション。
カメラは彼女のランニングスピードにぴったり追従し、疾走感・没入感・爽快感を最大限に強調する。
キャリーバッグを手放す瞬間も滑らかにつなぎ、アクションの連続性が崩れない自然な導線を重視する。
ライティングと色彩:
Crystal clear tropical daylight: 雲ひとつない快晴。太陽光は真上から降り注ぎ、海面はキラキラとダイヤモンドのように反射している。
Color Palette:
海の「シアン」「ターコイズ」「コバルトブルー」のグラデーション
空の「スカイブルー」
ヴィラの「ナチュラルウッド」「ホワイト」
彼女の衣装の「ピュアホワイト」
髪色の「ライトブラウン」
これらが彩度高めに設定され、視覚的な満足度を最大化する。
テクスチャと質感:
Water: 水は極めて透明度が高く、底の砂紋が見えるほど。飛び込んだ際の水しぶきは、一粒一粒がクリスタルのように細かく描写される。
Architecture: ヴィラの外壁は白い縦格子のモダンなデザイン。床のウッドデッキは、日光で乾燥した木の質感が伝わるようなディテール。
Wardrobe & Hair: 茶髪は南国の風を強く受けて自然になびき、白いへそ出しキャミソールとホットパンツは、開放的でヘルシーな夏らしさを強調する。
````

### 38. Seedance 2.0 15 秒一镜到底“觉醒冲击”提示词

**作者**: [ChrisTheNerv](https://x.com/ChrisTheNerv/status/2040043939109953944)  **日期**: 2026-04-03  **语言**: zh

> 一份极其详尽的 Seedance 2.0 15 秒一镜到底提示词，描述了一位中国美女在末日城市中变身为装甲战士的电影级场景，涵盖了具体的运镜方式、音效设计及物理真实感要求。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/28a539813b37484f2f914d1836be4102/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/28a539813b37484f2f914d1836be4102/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
100%真人实拍质感，好莱坞IMAX大片质感，自然光影，冷峻纪实风格，阴天自然光，全程手持一镜到底，呼吸感晃动，随机焦点失焦，16:9宽屏。
【场景环境】
一条延伸至远方的被摧毁的城市街道。两侧是废墟混凝土建筑，钢筋外露，窗户破碎，部分建筑仍在燃烧，橙色火光与黑烟升腾。废弃汽车散落在开裂的沥青路面上，其中数辆正在燃烧。阴沉灰色天空，烟尘悬浮于空气中。多颗陨石拖着火焰与浓烟尾迹划过天际。背景中惊恐的平民在废墟间四散奔逃，有人跌倒，有人拖拽伤员。
【主体人物】
中国美女，深红色头发扎成松散凌乱的发髻，几缕发丝垂在脸旁。皮肤白皙，五官锋利，下颚线分明，自然妆容，眼妆细致。着装：黑色长款皮革风衣内搭黑色背心，黑色牛仔超短裙，黑色平底战斗靴，无腰带，双手佩戴黑色科技感护手。表情紧绷隐忍，微带痛苦，眉头微蹙——眼神中充满绝望与强烈的意志。
【15秒一镜到底·觉醒打击版】
0-2秒·觉醒
镜头低角度仰拍，取景她的上半身与面部，仰望独自站在被摧毁街道中央的她。风吹动她的黑色皮革风衣。她张开嘴唇，用日语尖叫:"かくせいしろ！"她猛然张开右手，黑色科技护手噼啪作响。紫色水晶质感的电弧从她手臂和护手爆发。空气向内压缩，空间扭曲畸变。冲击波发出低沉的音爆。紫色符文线条浮现并环绕她身体运转。
2-5秒·爆发
镜头开始环绕她运动。胸口爆裂出暗金色裂纹，浓稠的金色液体如血般涌出。她痛苦地尖叫。紫色雾气与细密电弧向外涌射。她的全部衣物从内部撕裂炸开，每一片都燃烧成灰烬——什么都不剩。有机装甲碎片向外爆射，随后以不自然的方式回缩重新附着在她身体上。紫色纹路对称蔓延过她的面部。面颊上裂开一道裂缝，露出下方脉动的紫色光芒。同时，多条机械臂状的附肢从她背部猛烈爆出——暗色金属质感，刀刃形状，如恶魔之翼般向外展开。火花、蓝色电弧和金色能量粒子从爆发点炸裂。镜头从背后捕捉完整的展开画面——她的剪影映衬在灰色天空下，机械附肢如扇形展开。爆发声如撕裂金属混合电弧放电。
5-8秒·生长
有机物质从体内渗出，表面闪烁虹彩光泽。白色装甲板对撞融合，留下灼烧痕迹。装甲向下延伸覆盖她的双腿，平底战斗靴被装甲完全吞噬取代，形成白色与暗紫色交织的装甲战靴，伴随微小火花锁定到位。她咬紧牙关发出痛苦的嘶吼。胸口核心如余烬般明灭闪烁。紫黑色金属蔓延覆盖她的面部，形成凹凸不平的面具，左眼比右眼先被覆盖。复眼开始成型，带有液态光介质不规则地闪烁。镜头持续环绕她运动。
8-12秒·完成
镜头继续缓慢环绕她。面具完全封合。角状结构从头顶向上生长，燃烧着紫金色火焰。一只复眼稳定发光，另一只带有电流不稳定的闪烁。装甲以白色与暗紫色交织，凹凸不平且布满战损，发光的紫色裂缝中渗出光液。机械附肢在她身后微微摆动。装甲每块锁定时发出清脆的金属卡扣声，随后是层次分明的机械归位声。她缓缓低头审视自己的双手——白色与暗紫色交织的装甲护手指节渗出紫色光芒。她缓缓抬头直视前方，复眼骤然全亮。
12-15秒·超音速冲锋
镜头急速后退。她双脚蹬地，脚下沥青瞬间炸裂形成深坑，一道猛烈的紫色能量爆炸从起飞点向外扩散，碎石与沥青碎块被炸飞至空中。她以突破音障的速度腾空飞射，直冲镜头方向——锥形音爆雾气在身后形成，机械附肢被气流向后压平，画面产生强烈的动态模糊。她的身影越来越大，越来越近，占满整个画面。紫色能量尾迹拖在身后。最后一帧，她的装甲面甲几乎撞上镜头，复眼猩红全亮，画面骤然切黑。
【环境音】
觉醒时的低沉音爆，撕裂金属与电弧放电声，痛苦的尖叫声，清脆的金属卡扣声，机械附肢展开的沉重金属声，背景中燃烧的噼啪声与远处爆炸声，最后的超音速冲锋伴随起飞点爆炸声、音爆冲击与急速逼近的风压声，画面切黑瞬间一切归于寂静。
【物理质感强化】
真实光影，变身前面部可见的皮肤质感，皮革风衣变身前可见的真实磨损与撕裂。机械附肢具有物理重量和惯性——展开后轻微摆动，并非僵硬不动。装甲板以白色与暗紫色交织，表面可见划痕、焊接痕迹和不平整边缘——不是干净光滑的。所有动作沉稳有力，充满痛苦但坚定——她在承受中觉醒。偶有轻微镜头晃动，纯正手持跟拍感。
【声音设计】
从尖叫激活到爆裂机械爆发，层层递进至起飞点爆炸与超音速冲锋的音爆，最终骤然切入寂静。整个序列散发着绝对的力量。仅生成音效，无音乐。
````

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/8c591505bff6677a20938f04c02b8e2d/watch)

**Prompt:**
````
【云窟剑影·天门血战】
——张家界天门山一镜到底
核心风格： 徐克新式武侠大片、一镜到底、高帧率、4K超清。

色调： 徐克亮调，“冷玉青墨 + 琥珀流光”。高对比、山岚自带柔光滤镜，锐化人物轮廓，达芬奇工业级调色。

场景： 张家界天门山（湘西诡谲地貌。天门洞开，吞云吐雾；999级天梯垂直挂于绝壁，如通天之路；石林石柱如利剑攒蹙，云海翻腾间栈道若隐若现，飞鸟不渡）。

运镜轨迹：
低角度仰拍（强调天险） → 急速推向洞口 → 180°横向平移（展现栈道激斗） → 俯冲下坠 → 缓拉回正 → 逆光特写。

镜头脚本：
0-4秒【起势·天门云涌】：

运镜： 极低角度仰拍，镜头从天梯底部向上急速俯冲掠过。

画面： 人物面部参考@【@图1】武侠侠客装扮（白衣胜雪，斗笠压低，手持长剑） 孤身立于999级天梯中央。

动作： 狂风卷起周遭云雾，【@图1】右手扶剑柄，左手捏剑指划过鼻梁。镜头拉远，展现其背后的天门洞，宛如一只巨大的苍天之眼。

4-8秒【激斗·悬梯截杀】：

运镜： 180°环绕平移。

画面： 十余名劲装死士从两侧如猿猴般贴着绝壁荡下。

动作： 【@图1】足尖点梯，身形倒挂旋转。（徐克式慢动量感） 剑不出鞘，以鞘代棍点、拨、挑，气浪将台阶上的雨水震成水雾。镜头急速环绕，捕捉残影与金属撞击的火花。

8-11秒【破阵·纵横石林】：

运镜： 镜头跟随人物俯冲，穿过石拱门进入悬崖栈道。

画面： 刺客布下钢丝阵。

动作： 【@图1】长剑终于出鞘（剑身映射琥珀色日光），一记横扫千军。剑气化作青墨弧光，斩断钢丝，钢丝崩断回弹击碎崖石。他在仅容一人的栈道上闪转腾挪，身影与石柱交错，虚实结合。

11-15秒【收势·雾散孤峰】：

运镜： 镜头从洞口向外缓拉，由窄变宽，展现万丈深渊。

画面： 漫天符纸（或枯叶）随风飞舞，【@图1】立于天门洞边缘，脚下即是云海。

动作： 挽剑花归鞘，反手背剑。阳光从天门洞背后透射过来，形成巨大的丁达尔效应。

定格： 镜头推进至极度特写，斗笠边缘滴下一滴血，划过下颌。眼神凌厉如电，背景是无尽的山河大观。
````

The camera tilts violently over the edge, staring straight down at the 1000-foot abyss. He lets out a sharp, panicked gasp. For a terrifying second, his body leans into the void, but he desperately claws at the pole with his fingers, his boots scrambling against the side until he manages to hook his leg and haul himself back up.

````
Jump 4: Still trembling, he forces a frantic, heavy-breathing leap to the next bar to keep the momentum.

Jump 5: A final, explosive long-distance jump to a swaying metal platform. He lands with a heavy, jarring metallic 'Clang', his body hunching low, gripping the vibrating metal for dear life.

[The Ending]
The camera remains in a low, fetal position on the final bar, shaking from the adrenaline. No dialogue. The audio is a visceral layer of the aggressive 'Hyuo' wind, his intense, ragged, and rapid gasping for air, and a loud, thumping heartbeat that resonates as if inside his chest. ### 52. 电影预告片风格视频生成
````

**作者**: [頓花聖太郎｜YAMI](https://x.com/tonka1981jp/status/2038854904899665941)  **日期**: 2026-03-31  **语言**: en

> 这是一个为 Seedance 2.0 设计的详细多镜头提示词，用于创作电影预告片风格的视频。该提示词明确了摄像机运动、场景过渡（从插画到写实）以及整体风格参数。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/90bb0e183e1dac0008c30a786b52afdf/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/90bb0e183e1dac0008c30a786b52afdf/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
[0s–3s]: （ image1 ）A continuous slow push-in that never stops — zooming toward the center of a 19th-century Grimm-style storybook illustration of a deep dark spruce forest, As the camera moves closer, the illustration begins to malfunction, The trees sway in a wind that should not be possible inside a drawing. 

[3s–5.5s]: ( image2 ) The zoom continues without interruption. The illustrated begins to soften and dissolve from the center outward, as if a mist is seeping through the paper and replacing the drawing from within. As the camera keeps pushing forward, this zone of realism expands outward in a controlled, organic spread. The warm cream-sepia illustration gradually drains away into cold desaturated blue-green. The drawn surface at the edges briefly wavers and thins like damp paper giving way to moisture, then quietly dissolves into the same realistic forest texture. No abrupt morphing, no multiple competing distortions — just a single eerie replacement, as if the illustration is being overtaken by a real forest through a veil of mist. By 5.5 seconds, the camera is moving fully inside the real forest, and the drawing has completely vanished. 

[5.5s–11s]: ( image3 ) The forward motion gently eases into a continuous upward drift without a cut, as if the camera is being lifted through the real forest in one smooth arc. It rises between the trunks and passes through the lower branches, gradually clearing the canopy — not soaring too high, but just enough to reveal the breadth of the dark Nordic forest under flat grey light. The motion remains calm and deliberate, with a subtle floating quality, allowing the forest to breathe onscreen. The camera then begins a slow, natural transition from vertical ascent into a shallow backward glide, as if searching for the road beyond the trees. 

[11s–15s]: ( image4 ) The same movement continues seamlessly. The camera glides forward and gently descends out of the forest edge toward the road, settling into a low eye-level perspective near the tarmac. In one unbroken motion, it arrives at an extreme wide shot with the horizon stable and the road stretching dead straight into a grey-white vanishing point. The same boxy vintage sedan is already in frame, driving steadily away, growing smaller in the mist. Fallen pine needles drift faintly across the wet surface. The mist thickens gradually ahead. 

Global style: 35mm tungsten film, anamorphic, fine grain, cinematic. Desaturated blue-green midtones, crushed blacks, flat overcast diffusion. Smooth continuous camera motion, sharp details, stable horizon, natural proportions. First two shots transition from antique illustration warmth to cold cinematic realism. No text, no typography, no digital effects.
````

````
0:08-0:10

but he triumphantly walks straight into the perfectly clean fixed glass side panel next to it, not the open doorway.
````

**Prompt:**
````
Character & Setup
Full-body based on reference image (upper-body reference), with face, hairstyle, and features matched exactly. She wears a hat. Expression is tense and restrained, slightly painful, with a faint frown—carrying a strong sense of despair and intensity in his eyes.

Clothing: Dark grey coat, dark inner layer, no belt, wearing heavy black-tech gauntlets.

⸻

Visual Style

IMAX film look with a 35mm Panavision lens.

Low-saturation grey tones, compressed shadows with preserved detail, subtle film grain and edge vignetting.

Heavy, oppressive atmosphere with realistic lighting and physical presence.

⸻

Camera Rules

One continuous handheld shot with subtle breathing motion.

Starts from a low-angle upward shot, focusing on the face and upper body, slowly circling to a frontal view during transformation. The weapon in his hand remains the visual anchor.

⸻

0–3s · Stare

The injured protagonist stands still, slightly lowering his head. Her body is tense.

She slowly raises his right arm forward, stiff and heavy.

A dim glow surrounds the gauntlet. Her breathing subtly moves her body.

Suddenly, her eyes ignite with purple-white light, creating strong lens flares.

⸻

3–6s · Activation

A deep whisper: “Transform!”

She snaps his right hand sharply.

Purple crystal-like electricity bursts from her arm. The air compresses inward, distorting space.

A circular shockwave expands around her. Strange glowing blue runic lines appear and orbit his body.

⸻

6–9s · Tearing

Dark gold cracks erupt from her chest. Thick golden liquid flows like blood.

Blue mist and fine electric arcs surge outward.

Her coat tears apart from the inside, edges burning into ash.

Fragments of organic armor burst outward, then unnaturally retract and reattach.

Her face tightens in pain as glowing blue markings spread symmetrically. A small tear opens on his cheek, revealing pulsing orange light beneath.

⸻

9–12s · Growth

New organic matter seeps from within, shimmering with iridescent light and moving toward the chest.

White armor plates collide and fuse, leaving scorched marks.

The chest core flickers like embers, not fully stabilized.

Her outer clothing is violently stripped away.

Purple-black metal spreads across her face, forming an uneven mask.

Compound eyes begin forming, flickering irregularly.

⸻

12–15s · Completion

The helmet seals fully. Horn-like structures grow upward, burning with purple-gold flames.

One eye glows steadily while the other flickers with electrical instability.

Armor is uneven and battle-damaged, with glowing cracks and leaking fluid.

The camera slowly circles to her right, then pulls back from above.

She shifts into a ready combat stance, standing against the harsh environment.
````

### 73. 咖啡师 鲁布·戈德堡 机械

**作者**: [Joaquin](https://x.com/joaquin_arana/status/2036538635399692289)  **日期**: 2026-03-24  **语言**: en

> 一个极其详细的、多部分的提示词，用于一个 15 秒的视频序列，其中主角是一位手忙脚乱的咖啡师，他的咖啡馆是一个相互连接的鲁布·戈德堡机械。该提示词详细说明了角色外貌、环境、情绪，以及精确的动作时间线和可听元素，使用 Seedance 2.0 生成。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/e418e8fa61e4c95c9d1c9a7a579ed4fa/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/e418e8fa61e4c95c9d1c9a7a579ed4fa/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
SUBJECTS: Subject 1: A frantic barista — small, wiry, early 30s with permanently startled eyes and perpetual five o'clock shadow. Wild curly black hair barely contained under a brown newsboy cap. Wears a wrinkled olive-green apron over a flannel shirt with haphazardly rolled sleeves. Moves like a pinball — bouncing between stations, sliding across the floor, catching things mid-air without looking. Every movement triggers the next part of the machine. His body IS part of the mechanism. Pixar-style 3D rendering: rubbery expressive limbs, exaggerated squash-and-stretch on fast movements, warm skin tones. Subject 2: The café itself — every object is a component of one interconnected Rube Goldberg machine. The espresso machine is the central engine. The sequence involves: a marble track built from bent spoons along the ceiling, balanced cups on saucers that tip like dominoes, a hanging mobile of sugar cubes acting as a counterweight system, a toy train on a track delivering milk from the fridge to the steamer, and a small catapult made from a ruler and napkin holder that launches the finished cup to the counter. Subject 3: The customer — a deadpan woman in a business suit, briefcase in hand, reading glasses on a chain. Completely unfazed by the chaos. She stands at the counter with the patience of someone who has seen this before. ENVIRONMENT: A tiny corner café — barely ten feet wide. Exposed brick walls covered in chalkboard menus with hand-drawn coffee illustrations. Every horizontal surface has a mechanical element: marble tracks on shelves, cup-and-saucer balance chains along the counter, tiny pulleys strung from the ceiling with twine. Warm morning light streams through a single front window catching dust and steam. A small bell hangs above the door. The whole space feels like a brilliant inventor's workshop that serves coffee. MOOD: Manic joy. The barista is in his element — the chaos is intentional, practiced, musical. Every crash, pour, and launch is precisely timed. The punchline deflates the entire spectacle in the best possible way. TIMELINE: 0:00–0:03: The door opens — bell dings. The customer places her briefcase on the counter. Says nothing. The barista points at her, nods — he knows the order. He flicks a marble from his apron pocket onto a ceiling track. The marble rolls — clicking over ridges, banking around a curve, dropping through a funnel into a cup on a saucer on a high shelf. The cup's weight tips the saucer, pulls a string, releases a cabinet latch — coffee beans slide down a ramp into a hand-crank grinder. Audible: bell ding, marble clicking on track, cup clinking, string twang, beans cascading. 0:03–0:06: The barista cranks the grinder with one hand while pulling a lever starting the toy train. The train chugs along a counter-edge track — passes the fridge where a small arm places a milk carton in the car — continues to the steam wand where the track tilts and pours milk into a steaming pitcher. Ground coffee falls through a chute into the portafilter. The barista slams it in with his elbow while catching a falling sugar cube from the overhead mobile with his other hand, dropping it into a cup. Audible: grinder crunching, train chugging and whistling, milk pouring, portafilter clicking, mobile tinkling. 0:06–0:09: Espresso machine fires — rich dark coffee flowing into a porcelain cup. Close-up: crema forming, thick and golden-red, swirling. The barista steams milk — pitcher vibrating, velvety microfoam building. He pours with a practiced wrist flick — a perfect rosetta latte art pattern forms. He tops it with a single coffee bean placed dead center. Camera lingers on the completed drink — perfect, beautiful. Audible: espresso hissing, milk steaming (tearing-paper sound), the gentle pour, the bean placed with a tiny tap. 0:09–0:12: The delivery. The barista places the cup on the ruler catapult and slams his palm down. The cup launches in a perfect arc — camera follows in slow motion as it rotates, latte art intact, not a drop spilled. It lands with a clean clink on a saucer directly before the customer. Steam rises in a perfect spiral. The barista slides into frame behind the counter, slightly breathless, fingers pointing at the drink with showman's pride. Audible: catapult snap, cup whistling through air, clean landing clink, a beat of silence. 0:12–0:15: The customer adjusts her reading glasses. Looks at the latte art. Looks at the barista. "Actually — can I get tea?" The barista's face falls — completely deflated. Shoulders drop. Cap slides askew. A long beat. Then his eyes snap back to life. He pulls out a different marble — a green one — and flicks it onto a completely different track on the opposite wall. The entire café begins moving again — a whole new sequence activating. The customer takes a seat. She's done this before. Cut to black. Audible: her flat delivery, the defeated exhale, then the green marble clicking onto the track and the café machine roaring back to life.
````

````
Eastern action-comedy style, 15 seconds, one continuous take. Inside a simple wooden padepokan (traditional martial arts hall) in West Java with a strong Javanese mysticism (kejawen) atmosphere, an elderly inner-power master stands calmly at the center, wearing traditional black attire. His expression is humble and composed, as if he’s only about to demonstrate a light breathing technique. Four students step forward one by one with curiosity. The first student approaches—the master gently taps his shoulder with a single finger, and suddenly the student is blasted backward, rolling across the floor. The second student steps in; with a light touch on the wrist, he spins dramatically through the air and crashes to the side. The third student braces himself, but a soft tap on the forehead sends him flying far, sliding across the floor. The fourth student walks in confidently, yet with the slightest touch, he is thrown backward in an exaggerated arc, flipping past the wooden props of the hall. Each time it happens, the master pulls his hand back with mild surprise and slight embarrassment, as if he didn’t expect such powerful results. The camera shifts quickly between wide and medium shots, capturing fluid yet exaggerated action. The entire hall falls into stunned silence, everyone frozen in disbelief.
````

````
，1.7米，眉头微皱，表情坚毅，特勤黑色作战服，战术马甲，带屏控制器，服装有污渍划痕。 动作：行走中点击左臂控制器，激活全息投影，右手伸入投影穿戴红色机械臂铠，浅蓝色投影读条显示“SUCCESS”后熄灭，臂铠保留在右手上，控制器变为红色“START”。 （4-6秒） 核心画面：人物跃出船舱，在空中双手展开，0.5s转体旋转360度后保持滑翔、预备的姿态，激活启动指令。 动作：走到跳伞平台，向前跨出，0.5s转体旋转360度后双手向两侧完全展开，做出经典的巨型机甲变身前滑翔姿态。高速下坠中，点击左臂控制器激活“启动协议”（Protocol Start），伴随戏剧化的数字化浅蓝色调全息界面。 镜头：极速下坠拉近镜头，随后匹配人物速度保持距离，捕捉其滑翔预备姿态。 环境：海上万米高空，乌云闪电，海雾弥漫，能见度低 (6-8秒） 核心画面：机甲部件有序全息影像扩增变大，精确、高速地在人物周围组合成实体机甲中机甲各部件飞掠、组合的动作）。 变身过程（关键点）： 人物（比例1:47）在空中保持滑翔姿态，两套巨大的腿部和脚部部件（具有重工业机械美学，非方块）机甲全息虚拟影像从下方和侧面扩张蔓延，精确地附着并锁定在人物的下方，人物双脚踩入实体机甲。 两套巨大的手臂部件（包括保留的右手机械臂铠）和胸部核心部件全息虚拟投影变大扩增蔓延，精确地定位、对接并锁定，将人物身体完全包裹，外部实体机甲框架显现。 最后，机甲的头部和经典的V字天线部件从角色面部以全息虚拟投影变大扩增蔓延，旋转并锁定在顶部，形成实体机甲双眼点亮。 视觉：在部件全息投影扩张蔓延和组合时，有细腻的粒子对齐、机械锁定和能量释放效果，有炫酷的粒子和光线。 比例：人物（占比极小）完全融合在机甲核心内，变身过程流畅、有序、一气呵成。 镜头：仰拍，机甲框架占满画面。 （8-11秒） 核心画面：机甲组合完毕，在空中短暂停留并摆出经典的巨型机甲完成姿态，高速下坠准备着陆。 动作：机甲在空中组合完成瞬间，头部天线弹出，双眼点亮（产生镜头光斑），双手（特别是右手的虚拟/机械臂铠）做出经典的“完成”或“滑翔后准备”姿态。随后，机甲姿态转换，全身推进器点亮，高速下坠。 机甲细节：哑光涂装磨损掉漆，关节油污，推进器点亮，产生镜头光斑。 动态：高速下坠，边缘棱角发红发烫，留下拖尾轨迹。 （11-12秒） （保留原动作，重现重型着陆感） 核心画面：机甲如陨石般砸向海面，单脚跪姿单手撑地着陆，激起滔天巨浪。 着陆：机体悬挂压缩，回弹有厚重阻尼感。 海面：深蓝色海面被砸开，数百米高环形水墙扩散，水下水花与气泡漩涡，排山倒海的冲击力。
````

````
各環境に応じてライティングは動的に変化。風圧、スピード感、没入感を強調。

レール構造は常に一貫しており、変化するのは周囲の環境のみ。

超高精細、シネマティック品質、滑らかな動き、リアルな物理挙動。

映像は停止せず、走行中のまま終了する。
````

### 88. 动作喜剧：酒店大堂里的老宗师

### 91. Seedance 2.0 机甲变形视频提示词

**作者**: [PlayForge AI](https://x.com/94vanAI/status/2034818230120849666)  **日期**: 2026-03-20  **语言**: zh

> 一个为 Seedance 2.0 设计的详细多帧提示，旨在生成一段逼真、电影级的视频，内容是一名特种部队队员进行高空跳伞并变形成一架 80 米高的重型机甲。该提示详细说明了视觉风格（IMAX、好莱坞橙青色调、重工业美学）、角色细节、环境（暴风雨中的高空海域）、摄像机运动（手持、跟随、低角度），以及机甲组装和最终戏剧性着陆的精确序列。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/39c0ac8062d7ececdf220991c56e77b8/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/39c0ac8062d7ececdf220991c56e77b8/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
核心主题：写实科技感，科幻机甲，磅礴史诗，重工业机械美学，真人演绎，极限运动
 
人物设定：

参考@图1，完全相同，身高1.7米，面部有微脏感；红色特勤作战服，高科技战术马甲，臂腕带屏控制器，服装和配饰有明显污渍、划痕与使用痕迹；深黑夜晚，光线偏暗，表情坚毅，眉头微皱。
 
场景与机甲：
未来感飞船船舱，海上万米高空，乌云闪电，海面海雾，能见度低；80米高重型机甲，真实金属质感，重工业机械美学。
 
画质与氛围：
IMAX胶片摄影，Panavision C系列镜头，动态模糊；好莱坞青橙色调，低饱和度，暗部细节保留，胶片颗粒感，轻微柔焦；写实科幻史诗风格，机械感与重量感，好莱坞级视觉特效。
 
镜头与画面：
手持一镜到底，轻微呼吸感镜头浮动；开场平视近景，后拉跟随，跳机变身时仰拍大全景，机甲落地后环绕过肩拍摄；人物激活控制器，穿戴虚拟机械臂铠，全息投影熄灭后虚拟臂铠保留，控制器显示红色“START”。

修改后：帧描述（动作参考巨大机器人变身）

帧1-3：穿戴与行走（0-4秒）
（仅作为前置状态）

核心画面：夜晚，未来感飞船船舱内，特勤人员在行走中激活控制器并穿戴虚拟臂铠。

人物：参考照片，1.7米，眉头微皱，表情坚毅，特勤黑色作战服，战术马甲，带屏控制器，服装有污渍划痕。

动作：行走中点击左臂控制器，激活全息投影，右手伸入投影穿戴红色机械臂铠，浅蓝色投影读条显示“SUCCESS”后熄灭，臂铠保留在右手上，控制器变为红色“START”。

画质：IMAX胶片质感，青橙色调，低饱和，手持轻微呼吸感镜头，动态模糊。

帧4-5：跳机（4-6秒）

核心画面：人物跃出船舱，在空中双手展开，0.5s转体旋转360度后保持滑翔、预备的姿态，激活启动指令。

动作：走到跳伞平台，向前跨出，0.5s转体旋转360度后双手向两侧完全展开，做出经典的巨型机甲变身前滑翔姿态。高速下坠中，点击左臂控制器激活“启动协议”（Protocol Start），伴随戏剧化的数字化浅蓝色调全息界面。

镜头：极速下坠拉近镜头，随后匹配人物速度保持距离，捕捉其滑翔预备姿态。

环境：海上万米高空，乌云闪电，海雾弥漫，能见度低。

帧6-8：组合（6-8秒）

核心画面：机甲部件有序全息影像扩增变大，精确、高速地在人物周围组合成实体机甲中机甲各部件飞掠、组合的动作）。

变身过程（关键点）：

人物（比例1:47）在空中保持滑翔姿态，两套巨大的腿部和脚部部件（具有重工业机械美学，非方块）机甲全息虚拟影像从下方和侧面扩张蔓延，精确地附着并锁定在人物的下方，人物双脚踩入实体机甲。

两套巨大的手臂部件（包括保留的右手机械臂铠）和胸部核心部件全息虚拟投影变大扩增蔓延，精确地定位、对接并锁定，将人物身体完全包裹，外部实体机甲框架显现。

最后，机甲的头部和经典的V字天线部件从角色面部以全息虚拟投影变大扩增蔓延，旋转并锁定在顶部，形成实体机甲双眼点亮。

视觉：在部件全息投影扩张蔓延和组合时，有细腻的粒子对齐、机械锁定和能量释放效果，有炫酷的粒子和光线。

比例：人物（占比极小）完全融合在机甲核心内，变身过程流畅、有序、一气呵成。

镜头：仰拍，机甲框架占满画面。

帧9-11：完成（8-11秒）

核心画面：机甲组合完毕，在空中短暂停留并摆出经典的巨型机甲完成姿态，高速下坠准备着陆。

动作：机甲在空中组合完成瞬间，头部天线弹出，双眼点亮（产生镜头光斑），双手（特别是右手的虚拟/机械臂铠）做出经典的“完成”或“滑翔后准备”姿态。随后，机甲姿态转换，全身推进器点亮，高速下坠。

机甲细节：哑光涂装磨损掉漆，关节油污，推进器点亮，产生镜头光斑。

动态：高速下坠，边缘棱角发红发烫，留下拖尾轨迹。

风格：重工业机械美学，真实金属质感，好莱坞级特效。

帧12：震荡（11-12秒）
（保留原动作，重现重型着陆感）

核心画面：机甲如陨石般砸向海面，单脚跪姿单手撑地着陆，激起滔天巨浪。

着陆：机体悬挂压缩，回弹有厚重阻尼感。

海面：深蓝色海面被砸开，数百米高环形水墙扩散，水下水花与气泡漩涡，排山倒海的冲击力。

画质：8K超细节，每滴水珠清晰可见，低饱和青橙色调，胶片颗粒感。

7、昂扬（12-14秒）

起身：机甲着陆片刻缓缓起身（史诗感）。翻涌的海水如海啸般冲击着机身，机甲起身的过程中，机体流出大量海水。巨大身躯在海浪中巍然矗立，海水只没过其膝盖部分，周围有如苍蝇般大小的直升飞机飞过，强烈的对比感凸显其难以置信的宏伟尺寸。机甲周身环绕着浓密的蒸汽和水雾，光线穿过产生丁达尔效应。直升飞机探照灯扫过机甲，金属表面产生霓虹反射效果。
 
7、威胁（14-15秒）
（保留原动作）
巨兽：机甲正前方远处出现一只体型庞大，散发荧光的海兽，对机甲发出咆哮。
````

````
第二幕：一段：15秒（机甲攻势·女侠破招） 画面风格全程参考1980年代香港武侠剧照质感：VHS录像带扫描线、胶片颗粒、褪色暖黄色调、轻微画面抖动。主角人物全程参考

：白色正装西服、机械义臂、金属颈甲、马尾发型、金色耳环，站立于废旧老爷车车顶，手持红色旗帜长矛。 分镜1（0-4秒）· 低角度全景 生成@图1末世荒漠场景，起始帧严格参照
图片1
构图——前景废旧老爷车占画面右下角，背景巨型机甲充满画面左侧天空。机甲胸口缓缓开启，喷出大股橙红色火焰直扑女侠；女侠单手持矛，另一只机械手臂抬起，从袖口喷出大范围防晒隔热白雾，与火焰正面对冲，火焰在白雾中逐渐熄灭，荒漠地面留下焦黑痕迹。镜头跟随火焰熄灭缓慢推进。 分镜2（4-9秒）· 跟随中景切换 机甲肩部导弹仓弹开，两枚导弹拖着白烟高速射出；慢动作特写导弹旋转飞行轨迹，镜头跟随导弹视角推向女侠；女侠侧身腾步，机械义腿抬起，一记侧踢将第一枚导弹踢偏，导弹击中远处沙丘爆炸；女侠旋身，长矛杆横扫击飞第二枚导弹，导弹在空中偏转后坠落远处哑火。切换仰拍视角，沙尘在阳光中飞扬，女侠稳稳站回车顶，白色西服下摆随爆炸气浪翻飞。 分镜3（9-15秒）· 三角快切对峙 机甲驾驶舱特写——驾驶员面部透过舷窗隐约可见，眼神震惊；切换女侠面部极端特写，眼神冰冷凌厉，嘴角微扬，金色耳环随风轻晃；切回低角度全景，女侠单手将红旗长矛缓缓指向机甲驾驶舱，沙漠热浪与黑烟在逆光中涌动。三角快切节奏逐渐加速，画面轻微抖动，VHS噪点加重，制造窒息对峙感。 仅生成机甲喷火轰鸣、导弹爆炸冲击声、金属碰撞声与荒漠风声，不要配背景音乐。动作设计符合武侠动作片规范，动作干净利落，禁止出现血腥画面，无危险动作引导，长矛长度全程与@图1保持一致。

第三幕：画面风格延续第一段1980年代武侠剧照质感：VHS扫描线、胶片颗粒、褪色暖黄色调。主角人物全程参考图
图片2
2。 分镜1（0-4秒）· 特写跟随起跳 贴地低角度跟随镜头，女侠机械义足在车顶蓄力，脚尖猛然蹬踏；切换侧面全景慢动作，女侠如离弦之箭从画面左侧腾空跃起，白色西服与红旗在空中猎猎展开，长矛矛尖直指机甲驾驶舱
图片1
，镜头跟随女侠跃升轨迹仰拍上升，天空、黑烟、烈日构成逆光剪影。 分镜2（4-8秒）· 被擒·僵持 机甲右臂机械巨手猛然横扫，一把将腾空中的女侠握于掌中；切换女侠面部特写，眼神凌厉毫无惧色，牙关紧咬，机械手臂被巨手压制，红旗长矛仍死死握在手中；切换机甲巨手特写，金属手指缓缓收紧，液压关节发出沉闷压迫声；再切回低角度全景，女侠被高举于空中，荒漠地面与废旧老爷车在脚下渺小如玩具。四角快切节奏紧凑，胶片颗粒加重。 分镜3（8-12秒）· 飞矛破舱 女侠猛然蓄力，机械义臂挣脱半步，单手将红旗长矛以慢动作奋力掷出；镜头切换长矛视角，跟随矛尖高速旋转向前飞行，划破空气直冲驾驶舱；切换驾驶舱内视角，矛尖刺穿装甲玻璃，驾驶员向后倒去；切换机甲外部侧面中景，驾驶舱装甲崩裂，内部火光迸发。全段慢动作与正常速度交替剪切，节奏爆发。 分镜4（12-15秒）· 机甲垮塌·定格 机甲双腿液压系统失控，巨手松开，女侠从高处自由落体；切换仰拍慢动作，女侠在空中翻身，机械义臂抓住垮塌机甲的残骸借力，潇洒落地，单膝点沙，白色西服沙尘飞扬；机甲在背景中轰然向后倒塌，爆炸火球腾空，黑烟遮天；女侠缓缓站起，背对镜头，面朝燃烧的机甲残骸，马尾发丝在爆炸气浪中逆光飘动，缓慢淡出定格。 仅生成机甲液压声、金属崩裂声、爆炸冲击声、长矛破空声与荒漠风声，不要配背景音乐。动作设计符合武侠动作片规范，动作干净利落，禁止出现血腥画面，无血腥暴力，无危险动作引导，长矛长度全程与@图1保持一致。
````

### 98. Seedance 2.0 电影级悬念提示词，附详细时间线

**作者**: [赛博杰尼](https://x.com/Merak1990/status/2033739319031308302)  **日期**: 2026-03-17  **语言**: zh

> 一个高度详细的 Seedance 2.0 提示，用于生成一个 15 秒、一镜到底、电影感十足且高度逼真的悬疑视频，背景设定在战后战场。该提示详细描述了场景、氛围、角色状态，并将镜头运动、声音设计和叙事进展分解为三个精确的时间段（0:00-0:04、0:04-0:10、0:10-0:15）。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/eee3cb1cfdaf2785ccfa6149684c6e85/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/eee3cb1cfdaf2785ccfa6149684c6e85/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
格式： 15秒 / 一镜到底 / 电影级写实 / 无剪辑、压抑且沉重的悬疑感、战后余烬环境音效设计 

场景描述： 战火刚刚熄灭的战场，能见度低，空气中弥漫着呛人的浓烟和未散去的焦味。地面被鲜血和战火浸透，满是破碎的旗帜、折断的兵器和层叠的战殁将士尸骨。一名身穿残破盔甲的将士，独自跪在一片狼藉之中，长枪插在血土中支撑着身体，盔甲上沾满血迹和烟灰，他的身躯仿佛随时会因寒冷和疲惫而倒下。观众应感受到强烈的凄凉感、窒息感以及仿佛被黑暗笼罩的紧张感，仿佛战火虽然熄灭，但某种更可怕的威胁仍在暗处潜伏。整个片段必须以一段不间断的、带有潜行感的运镜呈现。

 时间轴： 
0:00-0:04 | 铺垫： 低角度的潜行视角追踪镜头，穿过浓密的硝烟和零星的余烬。镜头不断被飞扬的焦炭颗粒和灰尘击中，形成忽明忽暗的视觉遮蔽。相机滑过一面沾满鲜血和泥土、印有残缺番号的破烂战旗，随后揭示出灰烬下堆叠的轮廓：一具被箭矢刺穿的铠甲，一个被半埋在土里的头盔。整体构图呈现出大卫·芬奇式的精准控制与信息留白。 音效： 狂暴的烈火残留声、烟灰摩擦金属的刺耳声、远方未散去的爆炸残响。

 0:04-0:10 | 升级： 镜头向右转动，聚焦于一名跪地的装甲将士。他以插入地面的长枪为支点，起初一动不动，唯有沉重的呼吸在寒冷中呼出白气。残破的战袍在寒风中剧烈抽打，铠甲上的血迹和烟灰随着身体的颤抖而碎裂脱落。镜头以几乎不可察觉的精度缓慢逼近并绕至其身后，不断收紧框架，拒绝提供任何安全感。 音效： 粗重的呼吸声、盔甲的嘎吱声、战袍剧烈的抽打声、埋在土下的残骸在风中发出的微小碰撞声。

 0:10-0:15 | 高潮： 越过将士肩膀，烟雾短暂变稀，一个庞大的身影带着沉重得不可思议的力量穿过黑色帷幕，其全貌始终未曾完全显露。将士感知到了威胁，恐惧地抬起头，呼吸急促，双手紧握枪柄，随后猛力拔出长枪。拔枪的动作将泥土和余烬扬起并甩向镜头，此时巨兽的轮廓在瞬间变得更加清晰。 音效： 沉重的踩踏声、烟雾风声骤降、急促的吸气声、钢铁挣脱血土的尖锐声、泥土和灰烬爆裂四散声。
````

### 111. Seedance 2.0 科幻机甲天使变形视频提示词

**作者**: [李岳](https://x.com/liyue_ai/status/2032097632576016622)  **日期**: 2026-03-12  **语言**: zh

> 一个极其详细的多段提示，用于 Seedance 2.0 生成一个 15 秒的单镜头电影视频，内容是一个角色在废墟城市屋顶上痛苦地变形为白金色机甲天使，强调逼真的 CG 美学、特定的摄像机动态（抖动、环绕、拉远）以及时间轴上详细的逐步动作和特效。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/2d46fc158b2a91575c8bd4878ae21b8b/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/2d46fc158b2a91575c8bd4878ae21b8b/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
【核心主题】
写实科幻特摄 ，废墟坠落 ，圣洁羽毛汇聚 ，白金机甲天使 ，电影级神性 

【人物基础设定】
面部有淤青，嘴角有血渍。表情略显疲态。
变身瞬间，表情轻微痛苦，眉心仅轻微蹙起，保持压抑感。 
白色破烂外套黑色随性破烂衬衣，和白色破裤子，经历了战斗的战损衣服。 
核心道具：
右手紧握一块散发着高频纯白蓝光芒的“圣环水晶核心”。 
场景环境：
末日，城市，摩天大楼天台，阴天，微风，战火纷飞，灰蓝色调天空。天空中划过带有火焰与浓烟的陨石。 

【氛围与画质】
视觉基调：电影质感。模拟 IMAX 胶片摄影机，搭配 Panavision C 系列镜头（焦段 35mm，光圈 f4）。 
色彩与影调：低饱和灰蓝主调。暗部信息压缩，保留细节。边缘添加轻微柔焦与适度的胶片颗粒感。 
风格核心：CG美学风格。强调生物质感与外星科技的融合，营造压抑、沉重、实拍的肉身痛苦感。 
特效核心：强调无数发光羽毛实体化汇聚的动态过程，以及机甲装备时带有神性。

【运镜】
单镜头：一镜到底，无剪辑。 
动态轨迹：开场极广角坠落 -> 震颤推至半身特写 -> 变身时环绕 -> 拉远仰拍全身。 
呼吸感：手持拍摄，全程保持轻微的、如呼吸般的镜头浮动，增强临场感。 

【时间轴】
0-3秒 坠落 动作：
主角从高空重重砸在废墟中惯性让身体滚了几圈，给人很惨烈的视觉冲击。身体激起环形烟尘气浪。她剧烈喘息着艰难站起，黑棕色头发凌乱，沾满泥污的脸低垂，目光死死盯着右手中搏动的蓝白色水晶核心。 
镜头：跟随坠落，砸地瞬间强烈震颤，快速推至半身。 

3-6 秒 羽毛汇聚 ：
主角喃喃自语低声坚定的说：“那就再来一次！" 
动作与特效：主角咬牙手捏碎手中的水晶核心。伴随清脆的能量爆裂声，一道刺目的白光冲天而起。
 羽毛汇聚：空气中凭空浮现出无数发光的洁白羽毛，它们形成一个高速旋转的涡流，瞬间包裹住她的右臂并迅速向全身蔓延。主角双眼瞳孔被纯白光芒取代。 
环境共鸣：身后浮现出一个巨大的、若隐若现的金色光环图腾。镜头因能量冲击产生耳鸣般的微颤。

6-9 秒 撕裂 ：
表情：轻微皱眉，忍受痛苦。 主角仰头承受巨大冲击，眉心紧锁。体内爆发出神圣的白色气浪 
核心：全身皮肤表面弹射出少许玻璃碎屑。金色光尘溢出，闪着彩虹色微光从腰带内侧向身体躯干蔓延。 
身体：白色烟雾从体内喷涌，裹挟着发丝般。 

9-12 秒 重组与展翅：
新物质：全套白色机甲覆盖全身，装甲表面带有珍珠般的哑光质感和金色的神圣纹路浮雕，缝隙中透出淡蓝色的能量光流。肩甲：新生的金色肩甲对撞，爆发出电光火花，留下永久的、如同烫伤的齿痕。 
羽毛核心展现：伴随着一声震撼的机械轰鸣，一对巨大的、由白色金属羽翼构成的机械翅膀在她身后猛然展开，翅膀边缘散落着发光的光羽。 
衣物：原有的衣物已经破烂不堪，被某种诡异的力量从主角身上快速抽离，离开身体。 
面部覆盖：白色透led碎面从面部开始蔓延面部，头戴由羽毛组成的皇冠，组成漏出面部的半透明头盔，头盔半透明面部显示屏中有生命体征和战斗信息的屏幕双眼。 
金色光环：背部有光纤量子生成圆形金色光环在背后浮现，白色金色色相间。金色光环旋转，旋转能量光脉冲式涌动。 视线：在整个变身过程中，主角的视线始终注视远方。纤细的金色电弧，发出滋滋碎响。身体周围的气流开始翻涌，翻涌的热浪对画面产生轻微色散畸变效果。 
装甲生长：伴随着富有神性的机械咬合声，白色的流线型机甲片在羽毛的光辉中实体化，迅速贴合她的躯干与四肢进行组装。金属连接处迸发出耀眼的金色电弧。
甲壳：甲壳碎屑四溅，有彩虹色棱镜碎片闪烁飘出，飘在身体周围，旋转悬停片刻后诡异回缩，重新回溯组合成战衣零件。 
面部：眼睛持续发白光，带有神性的威亚，面部出现对称的粗线条图腾纹身。 镜头：因冲击剧烈晃动、失焦，随即猛拉回正。 

12-15秒 完成 
头盔：整个面部被白色面具覆盖，只露出双眼。 
武器具象化：主角双臂向身体两侧猛然张开。掌心无数光羽凝聚，瞬间化作两把散发着白色烈焰的圣能战刀 
最终构图：镜头拉远并切为低角度仰拍。主角身着白金机甲，巨大的机械翅膀完全伸展，手持双武器摆出战斗姿态。她周身散发的神圣威压导致周围地面的碎石悬浮升空，画面定格在如天使降临般的震撼瞬间。 
最终镜头：环绕至人物右侧，机位变为俯拍，镜头以极缓速度逐渐向后拉远，变身完毕人物向正上方弹射起飞，垂直飞出画面。镜头被巨大的气流和热浪影响而抖动。
````

> 为 Seedance 2.0 提供的详细中文提示，用于生成一部连续、一镜到底的武侠史诗视频，视觉美学风格效仿徐克，强调高帧率、4K 分辨率、特定的色彩分级和复杂的镜头运动（低角度后方跟随、180° 环绕、穿过瀑布推入、缓慢拉出、特写定格）。该提示还指定了一个三段式动作序列（起始、破影、追影、收尾），并要求提供三张参考图像，用于角色外观和场景设置。

![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/6a5d85ad16bc93ace9c41193f5be9461/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
一镜到底，徐克视觉美学风格武侠大片，高帧率、4K超清； 色调：徐克新式武侠亮调，清透水墨青黛+鎏金高光，高对比电影感，山岚柔光锐化层次，达芬奇高级调色，干净凌厉高级感； 场景：绝壁千仞，千米大瀑布，图片3流泉飞珠、云雾环绕； 运镜：一镜到底无剪辑，低角度背跟→环绕180°→仰拍→推进穿过瀑布→缓拉→特写定格，气韵贯通； 0-3秒【起势·掠驿出尘】：低角度背跟， 图片1侧脸凝眸、眉目凌厉清冷，骤然转身镜头拉远；身着宋式青衣执剑立于瀑布水潭图片3前，足尖点水面掠出，指尖捻剑挥向苍穹，青锋剑旋舞化青影，飞身穿梭瀑布前，衣袂猎猎； 3-6秒【破影·扇退群敌】：环绕180°，白衣剑客图片2持剑追杀， 图片1后仰贴水面滑闪避让，青锋剑开合格挡化招；仰拍镜头下踏崖壁飞身腾越，借力飞升，剑影如青翼护体； 6-9秒【逐影·激斗】：快速推进+螺旋飞升，白衣剑客图片2俯身突袭， 图片1执剑凝气成锋，剑影化青幕格挡，气浪震碎瀑布、水花四溅；于绝壁间飞檐掠壁、辗转腾挪，青锋剑点刺劈扫，从容破袭；白衣剑客紧追不舍， 9-12秒【收势·收剑凝锋】：缓拉远景→仰拍特写， 图片1和图片2腾空跃立山峰之巅，黄金时刻的夕阳穿破云层，洒落在身上，勾勒出金色轮廓光影，背靠背静立，青衫和白衣随风飘逸，荷兰角，执剑归宗，青衫镜头定格脸部特写，眉眼冷傲，尽显侠骨风华。
````

![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/388e09d3cbcf9e9b0bd8fd1973212baa/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
Ultra-wide-angle macro FPV tracking sequence following a cat. The feline is never fully revealed; only fragmented glimpses pass the lens: the twitch of an ear, scattered whiskers, a paw brushing the floor, a swath of fur gliding past the camera. Focus continuously shifts between these fleeting details and nearby environmental hazards. Shot at 120fps to capture subtle tremors and high-frequency vibrations as the cat bounds and lands. Setting: An abandoned underground parking structure. Textured concrete floor, numbered pillars with faded, indecipherable markings, shallow puddles and tire tracks reflecting harsh light. Dust particles and condensation mist hang in the air. Sparse cold-white ceiling LEDs mingle with distant vehicle headlights, creating sharp contrast and deep shadows. The cavernous space resonates with emptiness and tension. Movement: The cat navigates unpredictably—darting through narrow gaps, executing sudden 90° pivots, explosive bursts of speed, and tight lateral rolls that skim edges of doors and guardrails. The camera mirrors its frenetic rhythm, micro-vibrating with the steps and accentuating exaggerated motion parallax as pillars and parked cars streak past. Key interaction: A gust of wind—generated by ventilation and a passing car—lifts loose debris: paper scraps, plastic bags, and dust swirl into a spiraling vortex. As the cat rockets forward, debris stretches into radial motion blur lines, enhanced by fisheye distortion. A rolling tire splashes a puddle, scattering droplets that refract light realistically. Climactic moment: A car’s headlight suddenly sweeps across the scene, reflecting sharply off the wet floor. The cat skids into a chaotic spiral, claws gripping the slick surface, fur vibrating, droplets flinging outward—captured in 120fps slow motion. Motion instantly resumes at high speed as the cat races along the ramp edge, hugging walls, and threads through a half-open maintenance door or narrow fence gap, escaping into safety. Atmosphere: Claustrophobic, urgent, and tense, yet ultimately triumphant. Sound design emphasizes rushing air, splashing water, metallic echoes from guardrails, and residual vibrations. The sequence concludes as the cat lands in a shadowy corner, with the camera’s lingering tremors gradually fading into stillness.
````

**Prompt:**
````
Harbor Break Run FORMAT: 15s / 6 SHOTS / grounded cinematic pursuit / no dialogue STYLE: Industrial harbor at blue hour, wet concrete, sodium-vapor lamps, soft fog, practical lens flares, restrained color palette, photoreal 35mm Shot 01 (0:00-0:02) A slow aerial drop into a working harbor reveals a single matte-black speeder blasting along a rain-dark service road between stacked containers and cranes. Shot 02 (0:02-0:04) The camera settles low behind the tail, close enough to feel the rear suspension vibrate; orange dock lights smear across the wet body panels. Shot 03 (0:04-0:07) A truck reverses unexpectedly across the lane, forcing the rider into a tight swerve through a narrow gap between a forklift and container corner. Shot 04 (0:07-0:10) The path cuts under a crane arm and through hanging chains, with droplets and sparks flicking off the speeder as it scrapes the edge of a steel barrier. Shot 05 (0:10-0:13) The camera pulls ahead for a front three-quarter angle as the rider exits the dock maze and skims beside open black water, city lights flickering across the surface. ### 117. Seedance 2.0 假面骑士变身咒语（黑暗特摄）
````

**作者**: [3vans](https://x.com/Magncsans/status/2030855387675754974)  **日期**: 2026-03-09  **语言**: zh

> 一个高度详细、多阶段的视频提示，用于 Seedance 2.0 生成一个 15 秒、单镜头、超现实的黑暗特摄（Special Effects）变身序列，灵感来自假面骑士。该提示详细说明了美学（昆虫仿生装甲、战损、荒凉废墟）、角色细节（忧郁表情、冷峻色调、面部/服装的特定参考图像）、电影风格（IMAX 胶片、Panavision C 镜头、低饱和度蓝灰色调），以及一系列复杂的动作和效果（凝视、激活、裂变、生长、完成），并伴有精确的摄像机运动（单镜头、缓慢环绕、呼吸式漂移）。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c834293167825e6b43745d82b1321cee/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c834293167825e6b43745d82b1321cee/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
写实暗黑特摄 | 昆虫仿生装甲美学 | 破损装甲 | 战损变身 | 荒野废墟 

【人物与基础设定】
面部：参照图片1上传图片，五官、脸型、发型百分百还原。保留暗色痕迹，可以美化，但面部整体偏冷感。表情全程阴郁。变身瞬间表情轻微痛苦，眉心仅微皱，拒绝昂扬斗志与眼神高光，保持压抑感。
服装：参考图片1，无腰带结构。佩戴哑光金属异形装置手套。
场景：荒野废墟，微风，空气中漂浮尘埃与烟雾，阴天荒原，灰蓝色调天空。远处天空偶尔划过带火焰拖尾的陨石碎片。

【氛围与画质】 视觉基调：电影质感，模拟 IMAX 胶片摄影机，搭配 Panavision C 系列镜头（焦段 35mm，光圈 f4）。 色彩与影调：低饱和灰蓝主调。暗部信息压缩但保留细节。画面边缘轻微柔焦，叠加适度胶片颗粒。
风格核心：暗黑特摄美学，强调生物机械装甲与未知科技的融合，营造压抑、沉重、真实的变身仪式感。

【运镜规则】 单镜头：一镜到底，无剪辑。 角度：开场仰拍人物左侧，聚焦腰部以上部位。 变身时镜头以极慢速度环绕至正面平视上半身。 完成变身后环绕至人物右侧俯拍。 呼吸感：手持拍摄，全程保持极轻微的呼吸式镜头漂移。 0-3 秒 · 凝视 动作：主角疲惫站立，略微低头，目光锁定手部装置。脊背紧绷。右手缓慢伸出。 镜头：极慢向前推进，捕捉身体呼吸起伏。 特效：双眼逐渐亮起冷白光芒。眼眶周围浮现细微能量纹路。 3-6 秒 · 启动 声音：低语「DESCEND」。 动作：右手抬起，轻轻打出一个清脆响指。 特效：响指瞬间，手臂被红色火焰包裹。空气向内塌陷形成扭曲。 身体周围扩散一圈半透明能量脉冲。 脉冲呈螺旋状扩散。 头发被扰动。 0.3 秒后能量消散。 身体周围漂浮出现不规则蓝色符号结构。 镜头：低频嗡鸣由远及近。镜头产生 0.1 秒应激震动。 6-9 秒 · 裂变 核心：响指爆发出暗红色能量裂纹。 红色能量液体沿着身体结构向躯干蔓延。 身体：暗红能量雾从体内扩散。 雾中夹杂细小电弧。 风衣：由内部开始撕裂灼烧。 碎片与能量雾一同飘散。 破口边缘逐渐焦黑。 装甲：仿生装甲碎片飞散。 碎片在半空短暂停留。 随后重新组合并附着回身体。 镜头：画面因能量冲击短暂失焦。 随后迅速恢复稳定。 9-12 秒 · 生长 新物质：全新的生物机械装甲结构从体内生成。 表面带有虹彩般光泽。 像活体结构般缓慢蠕动延展。 肩甲：新生肩甲对撞。 爆发暗红色火星。 留下能量刻痕。 胸甲：胸甲随心跳缓慢开合。 甲缝中闪烁微弱光芒。 衣物：原有外套被能量场从身体抽离飞出画面。 面部覆盖：粉白色薄膜从面部蔓延。 逐渐拼接成面具轮廓。 覆盖速率不一。 形成不对称结构。 复眼：多晶光学复眼逐渐亮起。 左眼比右眼快 0.5 秒完成。 部分单元闪烁。 亮度不均。 视线：整个变身过程中主角始终直视前方。 12-15 秒 · 完成 头盔：两只复眼完全组合。 整个面部被面具覆盖。 头盔顶部生长出冠状结构。 角部燃起蓝色能量火焰。 复眼持续发光。 部分单元仍有轻微闪烁。 肩甲：边缘翘起。 鳞片纹路明显。 缝隙中渗出微弱能量光液。 腰侧：一道巨大装甲裂隙尚未闭合。 暗红流光在其中流动。 随呼吸轻微起伏。 战衣：战衣呈纯白配色。 造型浮夸。 整体类似甲虫仿生机甲。 腰部、复眼与裂隙持续发光。 全身偶尔闪过细小电弧。 战衣表面布满战损痕迹。 最终镜头 镜头环绕至人物右侧。 机位变为俯拍。 镜头极慢向后拉远。 人物逐渐进入准备战斗姿态。 展示人物与环境信息。 结尾 风声。 无台词。 无爆炸。 无光芒万丈。 只有站立的人。 和不完整的装甲。 远处天空划过一颗陨石。 镜头定住。
````

````
[运镜]：中景镜头，Smooth Orbit缓慢环绕主体，保持人物始终在画面中心，模拟专业舞台直拍。

[风格/画质]：4K超高清，电影质感，消除翻拍噪点，锐度清晰，细节丰富，色彩自然真实，无闪烁，动作流畅无掉帧。

[约束]：人体结构正常，动作有发力点和延伸感，面部特征高度还原原图，画面稳定流畅，禁止动作像摆pose或做广播体操。
````

[cut] The chat responds — a grey bubble appears. He smiles. In stop-motion the brain shrinks slightly, a tiny gap appearing between brain and skull. He doesn't notice. He types again. [cut] Close-up of the skull interior — the brain is now a single tiny pink crumb rattling around the bottom of an enormous empty cavity.
````
First Act

10 seconds single continuous shot | Paris to Shanghai | Transforming Jet | Pilot Close Up

Single continuous take, camera tightly tracking the subject at all times.

The scene opens on the banks of the Seine in Paris. Thick smoke fills the air. Mechanical turrets thunder in the distance. The Eiffel Tower looms faintly through the haze.

0 to 2 seconds
A male pilot in a white suit is climbing dangerously along the exterior of a rapidly transforming fighter jet. He grips wing hinges, steps on folding armor plates, his movements intense and precise. The fabric of his suit flutters violently in the airflow. Tight close up on his face. Cold, focused, determined.

2 to 5 seconds
The jet, front facing twin engine fighter reference, skims just above Paris streets. Metallic transmission sounds roar as the aircraft begins aggressive transformation. Wings fold and roll into massive mechanical shoulder armor and blade like structures. Twin engines reconfigure into the robotic arm power cores. The fuselage splits open, revealing a cold metallic skeleton and glowing energy conduits. The pilot moves across the shifting exterior, then leaps cleanly into the reforming cockpit.

5 to 7 seconds
Transformation complete. A colossal humanoid mech stands in the Paris street, retaining tail fins and propeller inspired elements. The camera stays tight as it strides between Haussmann style buildings. The mech tilts its head upward. Back armor panels deploy, revealing a massive cannon. Orange red energy gathers at the muzzle. A beam erupts. A distant landmark shatters in drifting smoke.

7 to 9 seconds
The mech folds back into jet form. Engines ignite at full power. Twin orange red exhaust plumes flare intensely. The aircraft rockets upward. The Paris skyline shrinks rapidly below. Cockpit close up. White suit, black tie, eyes forward, fearless.

9 to 10 seconds
The camera pierces through clouds and transitions into low altitude flight over Shanghai streets. The Shanghai World Financial Center rises between Haussmann style buildings. The jet skims the road, twin engines scorching the pavement. Freeze frame.
````

````
Use case: cinematic sci‑fi action short (PG-13) Primary request: 12s, 16:9 (1280x720). Rainy night in a war-torn futuristic city ruin, cyberpunk neon. A fictional female agent (~30, short hair, wet face with dust) wears a black tactical exoskeleton with a blue energy pulse on the chest and wields a blue glowing energy blade. Timing / beats (hard cuts; keep the agent design identical across all cuts): 0–3s: low-angle rear tracking shot, fast sprint; raindrops hit the lens; neon reflections wobble in puddles. 3–6s: side tracking; she draws the energy blade; blue light illuminates her face; particles scatter through the light. 6–9s: brief slow motion; the hunter bursts from shadow; she leaps and slashes; sparks fly; rain is pushed into fine mist. 9–12s: close-up of the hunter shattering; debris + sparks + rain; rapid pullback to a wide skyline reveal; lightning flash lights distant damaged high-rises. Camera: large-format cinema look, controlled handheld; one clear move per beat; 24fps, 180° shutter, realistic dynamic motion blur. Lighting/mood: neon + blade as key, strong rim light, volumetric shafts through rain and fog. Color palette: cyan/blue energy, violet/magenta neon, wet asphalt gray, red scan eye. Constraints: no on-screen text, no logos/watermarks, no gore/blood, no real-person likeness. Avoid: flicker/jitter, warped anatomy, inconsistent outfit/face, overly noisy particles, overly fast unreadable action. Audio (optional): rain ambience, distant thunder, blade hum, metallic impact.
````

### 134. 好莱坞大片变形金刚场景提示（巴黎到上海）

**作者**: [John](https://x.com/john87445528/status/2025557080648581177)  **日期**: 2026-02-22  **语言**: zh

> 一个详细的两部分、一镜到底的 Seedance 2.0 提示词，用于描述好莱坞风格的变形金刚场景，其中有一位身穿白色制服的飞行员。第一部分描述了一个高速变形序列，从巴黎开始，在上海结束，重点是飞行员的动作和机械细节。它指定了 IMAX 宽幅构图、超逼真的 CGI、动态运动模糊，以及带有橙红色引擎火焰的冷蓝色调。该提示词包含对特定图像的引用（图片1、图片2、图片3），这些图像可能是场景元素的参考图。

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c80ae0bb328720ea38a26b5efc3fa98a/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/c80ae0bb328720ea38a26b5efc3fa98a/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
【10秒一镜到底｜巴黎→上海·变形战机·驾驶员特写】 一镜到底，镜头全程贴身跟随。场景开启于巴黎塞纳河畔（
图片2
），空中弥漫浓烟，机械炮台轰鸣，埃菲尔铁塔在烟雾中隐现。 [0–2秒] 身着白色西的男性驾驶员（
图片3
）在高速变形的战机机体外部惊险攀爬——抓握机翼铰链、踩踏折叠装甲板，动作紧张刺激，衣摆在气流中剧烈翻飞。镜头特写其面部，神情冷峻坚定。 [2–5秒] 战机（参考图2双引擎战斗机正视角）贴近巴黎街道地面疾驰，机身发出金属传动巨响，开始剧烈变形：机翼折叠翻卷成厚重机械肩甲与翼刃，双引擎重组为机械臂动力核心，机身蒙皮裂开显现冷冽金属骨架与发光管线。驾驶员在变形机体外惊险穿行，随后纵身跃入重新成型的驾驶舱。 [5–7秒] 变形完成，巨型机械人形屹立于巴黎街道，保留战机尾翼与螺旋桨特征，镜头紧贴其在奥斯曼式建筑楼宇间穿行。机体抬头，背部装甲展开，露出巨型炮管，炮口凝聚橙红色能量光影。能量光束轰然释放，远处地标在轻烟中崩碎。 [7–9秒] 机械人形重新折叠回战机形态，引擎全功率点火，双尾焰橙红炙烈，机体拔地而起直冲云霄，巴黎城市轮廓在下方急速缩小。驾驶员驾驶舱内特写：白西装、黑领带，目视前方，神情无畏。 [9–10秒] 镜头穿云而过，切入上海街道低空（
图片1
），上海环球金融中心在两侧Haussmann风格建筑间拔地而起——战机贴地飞驰，双引擎尾焰灼烧路面，镜头定格。
🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶🫶
第二幕：

10 秒一镜到底｜上海→旧金山・战机变形・帅气驾驶员特写】 一镜到底，镜头全程贴身跟随，机械运转声响清晰，上海陆家嘴金融区街道上弥漫着薄雾与橙红光晕。 [0–2 秒] 开场于上海场景 ——银灰机甲战机（
图片1
） 低伏于浦东高楼群间，东方明珠塔在薄雾中隐现，引擎尾焰呈现明亮橙红光晕。身着白色西装男性驾驶员
图片2
在战机机翼外侧惊险攀爬，抓握机身折叠装甲板，动作敏捷凌厉，衣摆被气流猛烈掀起。镜头推近其面部 —— 神情冷峻，眼神锐利。 [2–3 秒] 驾驶员纵身跃入开启的驾驶舱，舱盖以机械联动声平稳合拢。驾驶员驾驶舱内帅气特写：他单手握杆，另一只手缓缓向后捋起发丝，嘴角微扬，眼神望向远方，气流吹动西装领口，极致帅气。 [3–5 秒] 战机引擎全功率点火，双尾焰橙红明亮，机体从上海街道拔地垂直跃升，陆家嘴天际线在下方急速后退缩小。镜头跟随机腹仰视，穿云破雾，太平洋蔚蓝海面在云层下方铺展。 [5–7 秒] 金门大桥红色钢塔从云雾中拔地而起，旧金山湾区城市轮廓隐现。战机贴近桥面平稳掠过，气流将桥面尘埃与微光粒子卷起。机身开始流畅变形：机翼折叠翻卷成厚重机械肩甲与翼刃，引擎重组为动力核心与机械底盘，机身蒙皮自然过渡显现冷冽金属骨架与发光管线，四轮从机腹展开触地 —— 数秒内化为银灰超级机械赛车（
图片3
），轮拱带有明亮粒子效果。 [8–10 秒] 变形完成，机械赛车在金门大桥桥面全速冲刺，驾驶员清晰可见于透明座舱内，双手紧握方向盘，车身擦地飞驰、粒子闪烁，旧金山湾区全景在背景中展开。镜头从侧后方低角度跟拍，定格于速度与钢铁的极致张力中。 风格标签：超写实 CGI、电影级动态模糊与运动拖影、冷蓝灰城市色调、橙红引擎焰光、无剪辑一镜到底、IMAX 宽幅构图、金属传动音效全程。
````

**视频**: [观看视频](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/6c45dd501929d908b66c901810d0435c/watch)
![缩略图](https://customer-qs6wnyfuv0gcybzj.cloudflarestream.com/6c45dd501929d908b66c901810d0435c/thumbnails/thumbnail.jpg)

**Prompt:**
````
ARGUMENT - WHIP PAN FOLLOWS SPEAKER
15 Seconds / Continuous Shot / Dynamic Camera

SHOT DESCRIPTION:

Interior. Apartment. Day. WOMAN (30s) and MAN (32) mid-argument. Camera WHIP PANS to follow WHOEVER IS SPEAKING. Clean sequence, no character appears twice in same position.

0:00-0:02
Woman near door.

WOMAN
You promised. You said you'd be here.

0:02-0:04
WOMAN (CONT'D)
Our appointment was at three o'clock.
Where were you?

She steps forward.

Man turns away.

MAN
I got held up at work. It's not a big deal.

0:04-0:06
Eyes wet but controlled anger.

WOMAN
Not a big deal? I took off work.
I rearranged everything.

Shoulders tense. He responds.

MAN
You think I don't know that?
You think I don't feel like shit about it?

0:06-0:08
Voice drops, sharper.

WOMAN
Feeling like shit doesn't change anything.
It doesn't undo it.

man moves toward her. Defensive posture breaking.

MAN
What do you want from me? An apology?
Fine. I'm sorry.

0:08-0:10
Her face hardens. Sadness beneath anger.

WOMAN
I don't want apologies anymore, David.

man stops moving. Her words hit different.

WOMAN (CONT'D)
(from off-screen, but camera on man)
I want you.

Silence stretches. His face changes.

0:10-0:12
Man opens mouth to respond.

OVERSHOOTS past woman, continues past apartment door into hallway beyond.

0:12-0:15
WHIP PAN CONTINUES, unmotivated, chaotic, through open doorway across hallway.

Lands on: Apartment door cracked open. Inside: GOLDEN RETRIEVER PUPPY (4 months, fluffy, confused).

PUPPY's head tilts. One ear up, one ear sideways. Looking directly at camera. Confused. Concerned. Like it heard the argument and doesn't understand why two humans are sad.

HOLD on puppy's face. Blinks slowly. Eyes innocent.

SOUND: Argument stops. Only puppy's small breathing. Silence.

TECHNICAL:

- Camera: Whip pans ONLY, follow speaker's voice
- Pan motivation: Who is speaking determines camera movement
- Final pan: Unmotivated (emotional breakdown of camera discipline)
- 8K, Ultra High Quality

SOUND LAYERS:

0:00-0:04: Normal breathing, measured voices
0:04-0:08: Volume rising, frustration peaks
0:08-0:10: Emotion drops to sadness
0:10-0:15: Argument fades, puppy breathing only
````

> 一个详细的提示，用于生成一段电影般的视频序列，内容是一位剑客在月光下的竹林中。该提示详细说明了摄像机运动（360 度旋转、长镜头推近）、动作序列（拔剑、用剑气斩断竹子）和环境音效，旨在营造一种戏剧性的武侠电影风格。

**Prompt:**
````
月光下的竹林，一位白衣剑客站在竹林深处，衣袂随风飘动。他缓缓拔剑，剑身反射月光。镜头360度环绕旋转，竹叶纷纷落下。剑客突然出剑，一道剑气划破竹林，数根竹子应声而断。长镜头一镜到底，从全景推到剑客面部特写，表情冷峻坚毅。环境音：风声、竹叶沙沙、剑鸣。
````
